name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Executive Superior Twin Room
info:Stayed in July 2022
info:Friends
info:3 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted July 12, 2022
msg:I visited this hotel for a total of 3 nights over a couple of weeks. Each time I arrived late and left early. So to be perfectly honest I cannot give a thorough review of the Hotel and Amenities.
Check in was smooth, checking passports and health codes delays things, but it is a necessary requirement at the moment.
My rooms were spacious, comfortable and well appointed. I had views over the suburbs and one over the nearby buildings.
Breakfast was good quality buffet on the occasion I was able to eat. A wide variety of food options to suit all types of travelers. Do not anticipate a big plate of Bacon if you are expecting a Western full breakfast however.
Swimming pool was closed according to a disappointed travel companion.Downstairs bar area was often unattended. But there is a shop in the parking area just outside to the left, selling basic soft drinks and beer and snacks,  if you cannot get bar service.
Check in staff were friendly. Bed comfortable, but others in my group complained "too hard" or "too soft" that really is a personal preference.
Location, there is a huge shopping complex literally  outside the hotel, cross the car park and enter a huge complex (you will be on the 5th floor) that caters for almost any need that I could think of.
Restaurant area and night spots were a 10 - 15 minute ride away in a taxi. But there was what looked like a night market and Plaza at street level outside the hotel. I never got to check it out.
If I stayed at Urumqi again I would probably choose a cheaper  place closer to the airport. When all I needed was a bed the extra travel time and cost is not worth it. If staying several days I would choose this hotel again.
 That is honestly all I can contribute.
----------------------------------------
